    <script>
      $(document).ready(function() {
        setInterval(function() {
          $.get("/view-update?t=5e3107df3f3c185ec2d003efda2eb5ae82d5c1bd83ab9030504eb519d77cff09&offset=0", function (data) {
            data = eval(data);
            
            for (var i = 0, l = data.length; i < l; ++i) {
              var tds = $("tr[number$="+data[i][0].substr(1)+"] td");
              if ($(tds[4]).text() != data[i][2]) {
                $(tds[3]).text(data[i][1]);
                $(tds[4]).text(data[i][2]);
                $(tds[5]).text(data[i][3]);
              }
            }
          });
        }, 10000);
      });
    </script>
